Match Intro
At Estadio Nacional Julio Martínez Prádanos, Universidad de Chile will take on Coquimbo Unido in a Primera Division encounter set for December 2, 2025.

Universidad de Chile holds the 3rd position in the league, trailing behind Coquimbo Unido in 1st place, with 51 and 71 points respectively.

Universidad de Chile boasts an impressive record of 12 wins in their 14 home matches, while Coquimbo Unido has secured victory in their last 6 away fixtures in the Primera Division.

In their recent 6 head-to-head matches in the Primera Division, Universidad de Chile has suffered 3 losses.

Prediction: Coquimbo Unido to win by 2-1.

Match Intro
Brazilian League action returns as Vasco da Gama takes on Mirassol SP at the Estádio Club de Regatas Vasco da Gama on December 2, 2025.

With Vasco da Gama sitting at the 11th spot and Mirassol SP at 4th in the standings, the match promises to be an exciting clash between the two teams.

Vasco da Gama will aim to capitalize on their home advantage, having secured 4 wins in their last 6 home matches across all leagues.

On the other hand, Mirassol SP will be determined to overcome their recent away struggles, having suffered 4 losses in their last 6 away matches.

In their previous encounter, Vasco da Gama faced a defeat against Mirassol SP, adding an extra edge to this upcoming fixture.

Head-to-head stats favor Mirassol SP, having won their last encounter against Vasco da Gama.

With the stage set for an intriguing battle, the prediction for this match is for over 2.5 goals to be scored.

Prediction: Over 2.5 goals to be scored.

Match Intro
Sporting Cristal will clash against Alianza Lima in a Primera División match at Estadio Alberto Gallardo on December 3, 2025.

Currently positioned 3rd in the league, Sporting Cristal will face off against 4th-placed Alianza Lima in a crucial encounter that could potentially shake up the standings.

Sporting Cristal has amassed 31 points so far, the same as their opponents Alianza Lima, setting the stage for a closely contested battle.

The statistical data reveals Sporting Cristal's dominance at home this season with 13 wins out of 18 matches, while Alianza Lima has shown strength in their recent away matches, securing 3 wins in their last 6 outings.

In terms of goal statistics, under 2.5 goals have been scored in 7 of Sporting Cristal's last 10 matches against Alianza Lima, indicating a tendency towards low-scoring affairs when these two teams meet.

With the derby name Clásicos Callao - Lima adding an extra layer of intensity to this matchup, both teams will be eager to claim victory and improve their league standings.

Prediction: Alianza Lima to win with a probability of 37%.

Football is Mathematics. Forebet is a free data and analytics platform for football and sports predictions, using mathematical algorithms and statistical models to generate data-driven predictions. Аt Forebet, we analyze vast data to provide probability-based football predictions, match insights, and live statistics. Covering 1000+ football leagues worldwide, Forebet offers match previews, trends, and sports predictions.

Football is Mathematics. Forebet is a free data and analytics platform for football and sports predictions, using mathematical algorithms and statistical models to generate data-driven predictions. Аt Forebet, we analyze vast data to provide probability-based football predictions, match insights, and live statistics. Covering 1000+ football leagues worldwide, Forebet offers match previews, trends, and sports predictions.

Match Intro
On December 3, 2025, KS Burreli will face KS Luftetari at Stadiumi Liri Ballabani for a League 1 match in Albania.

The standings show KS Burreli in 7th place, ahead of KS Luftetari who occupies the 11th position.

KS Burreli has accumulated 16 points, while KS Luftetari has 10 points to their name.

Prediction: KS Burreli to win 1-0.

Football is Mathematics. Forebet is a free data and analytics platform for football and sports predictions, using mathematical algorithms and statistical models to generate data-driven predictions. Аt Forebet, we analyze vast data to provide probability-based football predictions, match insights, and live statistics. Covering 1000+ football leagues worldwide, Forebet offers match previews, trends, and sports predictions.

Match Intro
In a Premier League encounter, Rudar Prijedor will host Zrinjski Mostar at Gradski Stadion on December 3, 2025.

Facing off are 9th-placed Rudar Prijedor with 14 points and 2nd-placed Zrinjski Mostar with a comfortable 33 points.

Rudar Prijedor has struggled recently, losing 50% of their last 6 matches in the league.

On the other hand, Zrinjski Mostar has been strong on the road this season, securing 5 wins in 7 away games.

When looking at their history, Rudar Prijedor has faced difficulties against Zrinjski Mostar, losing 4 out of their last 6 head-to-head encounters across all competitions.

With our algorithm favoring Zrinjski Mostar to win with a probability of 66%, the visitors will aim to continue their impressive away form and secure all three points in this fixture.

Football is Mathematics. Forebet is a free data and analytics platform for football and sports predictions, using mathematical algorithms and statistical models to generate data-driven predictions. Аt Forebet, we analyze vast data to provide probability-based football predictions, match insights, and live statistics. Covering 1000+ football leagues worldwide, Forebet offers match previews, trends, and sports predictions.
